SELECT 
    h.event_id,
    e.data_date AS event_date,
    h.hr,
    e.venue,
    e.team AS team_1,
    e.opponent AS team_2,
    e.stime AS start_time,
    h.volte_attempts AS calls,
    h.volte_mou AS call_minutes,
    h.lte_dl_rlc_gb + h.lte_ul_rlc_gb AS lte_4g_data_usage_gb,
    g.dl_maclayer_datavol_mb + g.ul_maclayer_datavol_mb AS _5g_data_usage_mb
FROM 
    vpt_hourly h
JOIN 
    vpt_event_schedules e ON h.event_id = e.event_id
LEFT JOIN 
    vpt_hourly_5gpt g ON h.event_id = g.event_id AND h.data_date = g.data_date AND h.hr = g.hr
WHERE 
     e.data_date >= '2025-03-01'
ORDER BY 
    e.data_date DESC, e.stime, h.hr
LIMIT 100;
